class=\"modal-body scrollbox\">\n                    <h2>Please note, our opening hours over Easter are slightly different:</h2><h2>\n</h2><h3>\nFri 14th April -  Closed<br>\nSaturday 15th April - 8:00am - 12:30pm<br>\nSunday 16th April - 10am - 4:30pm<br>\nMonday 17th April - 8am - 9:15pm<br> \nTuesday 25th April -  8am - 9:15pm <br><br>\n</h3>\n<div class=\"faq\">\n    <h3>How it works</h3>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Are you a subscription service?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Yes, we are a weekly subscription service, but there is no minimum term, and you can change your deliveries to fit with your lifestyle. The cut-off for subscription adjustments (pauses, cancellations, order restarts, address and box type changes)\n            made through the online customer <a href=\"/customer/account/login/\" target=\"blank\">login</a> is <b>11:59PM (Sydney time) on the Wednesday</b> before your next delivery, and if you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday.\n            <br> To find out more, go to <a href=\"http://www.hellofresh.com.au/managingsubscriptions/\">Manage your subscription</a>.\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Is there a minimum subscription length?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Nope, there is no minimum term, just remember to <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/customer/account/login/\">login</a> and make the changes to your account before Wednesday 11:59PM (Sydney time) the week prior to your next delivery. If you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday. </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>\n            How do I deactivate my subscription?\n        </span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">\n           Cancelling your subscription is easy. Just make sure to do so by the Wednesday prior to the delivery by 11:59PM (Sydney time) via your online account, or by 4PM if you'd like Customer Care to make the change on your behalf.<br><br>\n\nTo cancel online yourself, just need to follow these steps:<br>\n            <ul>\n                <li>1. <a href=\"/customer/account/login/\" target=\"blank\">Login</a> to your online account and click on your name at the top right corner, and select <b>Settings.</b></li>\n                <li>2. Scroll down and click on <b>deactivate my subscription</b> in the bottom right hand corner. Please note that if you also have a fruit box or multiple subscriptions, you will need to go through two cancellation processes- these can be navigated between using the green tabs above <b>Subscription info</b> at the top of the page, which are named based on the box type.</li>\n                <li>3. Follow the steps to cancel, which allows you to choose to <b>deactivate right away</b> or select a last delivery date.</li>\n                <li>4. Complete the short survey and let us know what you think of your HelloFresh experience!l</li>\n                <li>5. Once you complete the process, you will receive an email confirming your cancellation was successful. Please contact us if you do not receive an email confirming your cancellation, as it may not have been successful.</li>\n\n            </ul>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Can I put my subscription on pause?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Yes you can. If you're travelling or would like to hold your subscription for any reason, simply <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/customer/account/login/\">login</a> to your account, and the 'My Deliveries' tab will load. From there, you can see a calendar on the top right of the page, clicking on this will take you to your 'Menu Overview', where you will see a calendar of your upcoming deliveries. Select the date you wish to pause and click 'Skip week', the date will then turn red.If you have more than one HelloFresh subscription, you will see both subscriptions in the calendar when you click on the date you wish to pause, so remember to skip all subscriptions if you don't wish to receive any deliveries on this day. Just make sure that you make these changes before Wednesday 11:59PM (Sydney time) prior to the following week's delivery, and if you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday. For detailed instructions go to <a href=\"http://www.hellofresh.com.au/managingsubscriptions/\">How to Manage Your Account</a>\n</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>How much will I be charged each week?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">\n           This will change depending on what box size and type you choose, so please refer <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/food-boxes/\">here</a>.\n            <br>Delivery is usually free, or a small fee for premium delivery windows.\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>When will I be charged?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Once you sign up for your first <a href=\"/food-boxes/\" target=\"blank\">HelloFresh box</a> you will be charged right away. For all subsequent deliveries you will be charged after orders are confirmed and before orders are dispatched, usually on Thursday. Please allow a few days for the charge to show on your account. If the payment doesn't go through, you will be sent an invoice.</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>What happens if I receive an invoice?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Once you receive an invoice you must make payment according to the instructions on the invoice. We are unable to reattempt to charge your card for a delivery associated with an invoice that has been generated.</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <h3>Manage your account</h3>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Can I change to another box?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">You can always change your box type (Classic, Vegetarian or Family), number of meals, and number of people. Just <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/customer/account/login/\">login</a> to your account, click on your name at the top of the screen and then 'Settings' and make your changes.   If you have more than one subscription, for example, a meal box and a fruit box, you will need to manage these accounts separately. Just make sure you update your order before 11:59PM (Sydney time) Wednesday (Sydney time) prior to the following week's delivery, and if you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday..</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>What if I change my address?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Let us know as soon as you can. To update your delivery details, <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/customer/account/login/\">login</a> to your account and  click on your name at the top of the screen and then 'Settings' and make your changes.   If you have more than one subscription, for example, a meal box and a fruit box, you will need to manage these accounts separately. Just make sure you update your order before 11:59PM Wednesday (Sydney time) prior to the following week's delivery, and if you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday. We are always expanding our delivery area, so if we don't deliver to you yet, check back<a href=\"http://www.hellofresh.com.au/aboutus_delivery_areas/\">here</a>                for future updates! </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>When do you deliver?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Orders made before Wednesday 11:59PM (Sydney time) will be delivered the following week. If you head to the checkout and enter your postcode you can see a full list of the delivery window options in your area!</div>\n    </div>\n\n  </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Can I request a specific delivery time?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">We cannot commit to a smaller delivery window at this stage and each week our routes are carefully planned based on the deliveries we have to make to be as efficient as possible. When checking-out, you can provide us with instructions on what to do if you're not at home to accept your delivery. In fact, most of our customers are not present when we deliver their food. Some customers simply ask us to leave their HelloFresh box in front of their door, while others tell us to take their box to a helpful neighbour or the receptionist in their building. Whatever your personal circumstances, our friendly drivers will do their best to find a way to make HelloFresh work for you. </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>What if I’m not home to accept the delivery?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Don't worry if you're not in - all of our boxes are packaged using specialty insulation and environmentally friendly cooling agents in order to keep your groceries fresh (whatever the weather), provided you are able to transfer the contents to your fridge on the evening of your delivery.\nIf you will not be at home, we can leave it in a safe place nominated by you. Please leave specific delivery instructions on the checkout page for our drivers to follow and we can help ensure your box arrives safely! To update these instructions, <a href=\"https://www.hellofresh.com.au/customer/account/login/\">login</a> to your account and click on your name at the top of the screen and then 'Settings' and make your changes. If you have more than one subscription, for example, a meal box and a fruit box, you will need to manage these accounts separately. Just make sure you update your order before 11:59PM Wednesday (Sydney time) prior to the following week's delivery, and if you'd like Customer Care to make any changes on your behalf, please get in touch by 4PM Wednesday</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>My box didn’t arrive, what should I do?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Let us know. Email hello@hellofresh.com.au or call 02 8188 8722. We will make sure that your box gets delivered.</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>I am missing something from my delivery, what should I do?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Make sure to double check the full length of your delivery window as your box won't always arrive at the same time every week.\nIf your delivery window has ended, let us know. Email hello@hellofresh.com.au or call 02 8188 8722. </div>\n</div>\n    <h3>Ingredients and cooking</h3>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Can I choose my meals?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Not at this stage. We sell standard boxes with exactly the same content which allows us to buy, pack and deliver in a very efficient manner. This in turn allows us to offer our product at a good price. Our recipe satisfaction scores suggest\n            that our customers are very happy with us choosing their meals for them! And, you can always view the upcoming week's recipes <a href=\"http://www.hellofresh.com.au/recipe/week/upcoming/\">here</a>.</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Do you cater for special dietary requirements?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Unfortunately not at this stage, since all <a href=\"/food-boxes/\" target=\"blank\">our boxes</a> have exactly the same content. However, the ingredients are separately packed and clearly labelled so there is the opportunity for you to omit or substitute offending\n            ingredients.</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Do I need any other ingredients, such as salt or olive oil?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">Yes, we assume you have a bit of a pantry. Things like oil, salt &amp; pepper, and some of the best-known cooking condiments like soy sauce, white wine vinegar, mustard, and perhaps even an egg or a little milk. We will always let you know what\n            the assumed pantry items are a few days before your box gets delivered to give you enough time to stock up.</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"acc_trigger\">\n        <img class=\"imgContent\">\n        <span>Where do you source your produce?</span>\n        <div class=\"textContent\">We provide our customers with fresh, high-quality ingredients while ensuring our suppliers get a good deal too!
